 It may also happen that there is pain in one leg or in one part of the leg

 There can be many reasons for leg pain
 kai baar anthan ke chalate, maance-peshiyon main akad ke kaaran, maance-peshiyon ke ek ke upar ek chadh jane ke kaaran, poshan kii kami ke kaaran, sharir main pani kii kami ke chalate yaa lambey vakt tak ek hi mudra main rahane kii vajah se taangon main dard ho jaataa he
 If the pain is mild then it will automatically go away in a few hours
 par dard bahut tej he or aaraam karne ke baavjood badhata hi ja rahaa haito turant doctor se sampark karen
